Generates the couplings for C Lambda values in J\+H\+U\+Gen and J\+H\+U\+Gen-\/\+M\+C\+FM. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em array\+Name} & This is the name of the array containing the coupling \\
\hline
{\em coupling\+Name} & This is the name of the coupling to set (should be unique for every coupling\+Index/higgs\+Index combination) \\
\hline
{\em coupling\+Index} & This is the index at which the name corresponds to the array \\
\hline
{\em higgs\+Index} & This is the index of which Higgs to use (M\+C\+FM supports 2 resonances) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
These coupling entries only have a real component. You can set them via\+:

Generates the couplings for spin 1 and spin 2 values in J\+H\+U\+Gen. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em array\+Name} & This is the name of the array containing the coupling \\
\hline
{\em coupling\+Name} & This is the name of the coupling to set (should be unique for every coupling\+Index/higgs\+Index combination) \\
\hline
{\em coupling\+Index} & This is the index at which the name corresponds to the array \\

\end{DoxyParams}
